# Frontend Specification Document

> **Version**: 1.0.0  
> **Date**: January 25, 2026  
> **Status**: Specification for Implementation  
> **Language**: English (Documentation) | Arabic (UI Labels, RTL)

---

## 1. Overview

### 1.1 Purpose

This document provides a complete frontend specification for the multi-service marketplace platform. It defines all screens, navigation flows, state management, and API integrations required to implement the frontend application up to (but not including) the booking phase.

### 1.2 Backend Implementation Status

| Module | Status | Notes |
|--------|--------|-------|
| User Authentication | âœ… IMPLEMENTED | Registration, login, OTP, password reset |
| ServiceType | âœ… IMPLEMENTED | Admin CRUD, public read |
| Partner Binding | âœ… IMPLEMENTED | Full lifecycle with state machine |
| ServiceItem | âœ… IMPLEMENTED | Partner CRUD, admin moderation |
| Booking | âŒ NOT IMPLEMENTED | Out of scope |
| Payment | âŒ NOT IMPLEMENTED | Out of scope |

### 1.3 Design Principles

- **RTL Layout**: All interfaces are right-to-left for Arabic users
- **Mobile-First**: Responsive design prioritizing mobile experience
- **State-Aware**: UI adapts based on user/partner state and permissions
- **Progressive Disclosure**: Complex forms broken into logical steps

---

## 2. User Roles

### 2.1 Role Definitions

| Role | Description | Primary Actions |
|------|-------------|-----------------|
| **Public (Guest)** | Unauthenticated visitor | Browse services, view items, search |
| **Customer** | Registered user | All public + save favorites, view history |
| **Partner** | Service provider | Manage items, view dashboard, update profile |
| **Admin** | Platform administrator | Manage all entities, moderate content |

### 2.2 Partner Lifecycle States

Partners have specific states that affect their UI access:

| State | Arabic Label | Dashboard Access | Can Manage Items |
|-------|--------------|------------------|------------------|
| `pending_otp` | ÙÙŠ Ø§Ù†ØªØ¸Ø§Ø± Ø§Ù„ØªØ­Ù‚Ù‚ | âŒ | âŒ |
| `pending_approval` | ÙÙŠ Ø§Ù†ØªØ¸Ø§Ø± Ø§Ù„Ù…ÙˆØ§ÙÙ‚Ø© | âŒ | âŒ |
| `changes_required` | Ù…Ø·Ù„ÙˆØ¨ ØªØ¹Ø¯ÙŠÙ„Ø§Øª | âŒ | âŒ |
| `rejected` | Ù…Ø±ÙÙˆØ¶ | âŒ | âŒ |
| `approved` | Ù…Ø¹ØªÙ…Ø¯ | âœ… | âœ… |
| `suspended` | Ù…ÙˆÙ‚ÙˆÙ | âœ… (read-only) | âŒ |

#### Conditional Action Buttons

| Current State | Available Actions |
|---------------|-------------------|
| `pending_approval` | Approve, Reject, Request Changes |
| `changes_required` | Approve, Reject |
| `approved` | Suspend |
| `suspended` | Reinstate |
| `rejected` | (No actions) |

#### API Mapping

| Action | API Endpoint | Method |
|--------|-------------|--------|
| Get Details | `/api/admin/partners/:partnerId` | GET |
| Approve | `/api/admin/partners/:partnerId/approve` | POST |
| Reject | `/api/admin/partners/:partnerId/reject` | POST |
| Request Changes | `/api/admin/partners/:partnerId/request-changes` | POST |
| Suspend | `/api/admin/partners/:partnerId/suspend` | POST |
| Reinstate | `/api/admin/partners/:partnerId/reinstate` | POST |

#### API Mapping

| Action | API Endpoint | Method |
|--------|-------------|--------|
| List Users | `/api/user` | GET |
| Get Stats | `/api/user/stats` | GET |
| Get User | `/api/user/:id` | GET |
| Update Role | `/api/user/:id/role` | PATCH |
| Toggle Verification | `/api/user/:id/verification` | PATCH |
| Delete User | `/api/user/:id` | DELETE |

---

#### Row Actions Menu

| State | Available Actions |
|-------|-------------------|
| `draft` | Edit, Publish, Delete |
| `active` | Edit, Unpublish, Delete |
| `inactive` | Edit, Publish, Delete |
| `hidden` | View Only (contact admin) |
| `archived` | Restore (if within 30 days) |

#### Dynamic Fields

The form fields under "Ø®ØµØ§Ø¦Øµ Ø§Ù„ØºØ±ÙØ©" are dynamically generated based on `ServiceType.itemFields` from the API.

#### Validation Before Publish

When clicking "Ù†Ø´Ø±" (Publish), validate:
- All required fields are filled
- `name.ar` is not empty
- All `required: true` itemFields have values

If validation fails, show inline errors.

#### API Mapping

| Action | API Endpoint | Method |
|--------|-------------|--------|
| Get Fields | `/api/partner/items/fields` | GET |
| Get Item | `/api/partner/items/:itemId` | GET |
| Create (Draft) | `/api/partner/items` | POST (state: draft) |
| Create (Active) | `/api/partner/items` + state change | POST + POST |
| Update | `/api/partner/items/:itemId` | PUT |
| Publish | `/api/partner/items/:itemId/state` | POST (action: publish) |

---

#### API Mapping

| Action | API Endpoint | Method |
|--------|-------------|--------|
| Get Service Type | `/api/service-types/:key` | GET |
| Search Partners | `/api/services/search?serviceType={key}` | GET |

**âš ï¸ BACKEND REQUIRED**: Currently, there is no direct API to list approved partners by service type with their public profile. The `/api/services/search` endpoint exists but may need enhancement to filter by `serviceTypeKey` and return partner-level data.

---


#### API Mapping

| Component | API Endpoint | Method |
|-----------|-------------|--------|
| Partner Items | `/api/services/:partnerId/items` | GET |

**âš ï¸ BACKEND REQUIRED**: There is no public API to get partner profile details (business name, contact info, serviceTypeData). The current `/api/services/:partnerId/items` only returns items. A new endpoint like `GET /api/services/:partnerId` is needed to return partner public profile.

---

#### API Mapping

| Action | API Endpoint | Method |
|--------|-------------|--------|
| Register | `/api/auth/register` | POST |
| Verify Account | `/api/auth/verify` | POST |
| Resend OTP | `/api/auth/resend-verification` | POST |

## 7. Screen-to-API Mapping Summary

### 7.1 Admin Screens

| Screen | Primary API | Method |
|--------|-------------|--------|
| Admin Dashboard | `/api/admin/partners/stats`, `/api/admin/service-items/stats` | GET |
| Service Types List | `/api/admin/service-types` | GET |
| Service Type Details | `/api/admin/service-types/:key` | GET |
| Create Service Type | `/api/admin/service-types` | POST |
| Update Service Type | `/api/admin/service-types/:key` | PUT |
| Toggle Service Type | `/api/admin/service-types/:key/status` | PATCH |
| Delete Service Type | `/api/admin/service-types/:key` | DELETE |
| Partners List | `/api/admin/partners` | GET |
| Partner Details | `/api/admin/partners/:partnerId` | GET |
| Approve Partner | `/api/admin/partners/:partnerId/approve` | POST |
| Reject Partner | `/api/admin/partners/:partnerId/reject` | POST |
| Request Changes | `/api/admin/partners/:partnerId/request-changes` | POST |
| Suspend Partner | `/api/admin/partners/:partnerId/suspend` | POST |
| Reinstate Partner | `/api/admin/partners/:partnerId/reinstate` | POST |
| Service Items List | `/api/admin/service-items` | GET |
| Service Item Details | `/api/admin/service-items/:itemId` | GET |
| Hide Item | `/api/admin/service-items/:itemId/hide` | POST |
| Show Item | `/api/admin/service-items/:itemId/show` | POST |
| Archive Item | `/api/admin/service-items/:itemId/archive` | POST |
| Delete Item | `/api/admin/service-items/:itemId` | DELETE |
| Users List | `/api/user` | GET |
| User Details | `/api/user/:id` | GET |

### 7.2 Partner Screens

| Screen | Primary API | Method |
|--------|-------------|--------|
| Register | `/api/partners/register` | POST |
| Verify OTP | `/api/partners/verify-otp` | POST |
| Login | `/api/partners/login` | POST |
| Dashboard | `/api/partner/items/summary` | GET |
| Items List | `/api/partner/items` | GET |
| Item Details | `/api/partner/items/:itemId` | GET |
| Create Item | `/api/partner/items` | POST |
| Update Item | `/api/partner/items/:itemId` | PUT |
| Change State | `/api/partner/items/:itemId/state` | POST |
| Delete Item | `/api/partner/items/:itemId` | DELETE |
| Get Fields | `/api/partner/items/fields` | GET |
| Profile | `/api/partners/me/profile` | GET |
| Update Profile | `/api/partners/me/profile` | PUT |
| Status | `/api/partners/me/status` | GET |
| Resubmit | `/api/partners/me/resubmit` | POST |

### 7.3 Public Screens

| Screen | Primary API | Method |
|--------|-------------|--------|
| Service Types | `/api/service-types` | GET |
| Search | `/api/services/search` | GET |
| Partner Items | `/api/services/:partnerId/items` | GET |
| Item Details | `/api/services/:partnerId/items/:itemId` | GET |
| Login | `/api/auth/login` | POST |
| Register | `/api/auth/register` | POST |

---

## 8. State Management

### 8.1 Global State

| State Key | Description | Source |
|-----------|-------------|--------|
| `auth.user` | Current authenticated user | `/api/auth/me` or `/api/user/me` |
| `auth.partner` | Current authenticated partner | `/api/partners/me` |
| `auth.isAuthenticated` | Boolean authentication status | Derived from token |
| `auth.role` | User role (customer, admin, partner) | From JWT payload |

### 8.2 Partner State Management

```
partnerState: {
  data: Partner | null,
  status: 'idle' | 'loading' | 'success' | 'error',
  permissions: {
    canLogin: boolean,
    canEditProfile: boolean,
    canManageItems: boolean,
    canAccessDashboard: boolean,
    canChangeServiceType: boolean,
    visibleToPublic: boolean
  }
}
```

### 8.3 UI State by Partner Lifecycle

| Partner State | Redirect To | Allowed Routes |
|---------------|-------------|----------------|
| `pending_otp` | `/partner/verify-otp` | `/partner/verify-otp` |
| `pending_approval` | `/partner/pending` | `/partner/pending`, `/partner/logout` |
| `changes_required` | `/partner/changes-required` | `/partner/changes-required`, `/partner/profile`, `/partner/logout` |
| `rejected` | `/partner/rejected` | `/partner/rejected`, `/partner/logout` |
| `approved` | `/partner/dashboard` | All partner routes |
| `suspended` | `/partner/suspended` | `/partner/suspended`, `/partner/dashboard` (read-only), `/partner/logout` |

---

## 9. Role-Based Permissions

### 9.1 Admin Permissions

| Permission | Description |
|------------|-------------|
| `admin.service-types.read` | View service types |
| `admin.service-types.write` | Create/update service types |
| `admin.service-types.delete` | Delete service types |
| `admin.partners.read` | View partners |
| `admin.partners.moderate` | Approve/reject/suspend partners |
| `admin.items.read` | View all service items |
| `admin.items.moderate` | Hide/show/archive items |
| `admin.items.delete` | Permanently delete items |
| `admin.users.read` | View users |
| `admin.users.write` | Update user roles |
| `admin.users.delete` | Delete users |

### 9.2 Partner Permissions (State-Based)

| Permission | pending_otp | pending_approval | changes_required | approved | suspended |
|------------|-------------|------------------|------------------|----------|-----------|
| Login | âŒ | âœ… | âœ… | âœ… | âœ… |
| View Dashboard | âŒ | âŒ | âŒ | âœ… | âœ… (read-only) |
| Manage Items | âŒ | âŒ | âŒ | âœ… | âŒ |
| Edit Profile | âŒ | âœ… | âœ… | âœ… | âŒ |
| Change Service Type | âŒ | âœ… | âœ… | âŒ | âŒ |

### 9.3 Route Guards

```
PartnerRouteGuard:
  1. Check if authenticated (JWT valid)
  2. Check if token is for partner role
  3. Get partner state from API or cache
  4. If state doesn't allow access to current route:
     - Redirect to appropriate state screen
  5. Attach permissions to context

AdminRouteGuard:
  1. Check if authenticated (JWT valid)
  2. Check if user role = 'admin'
  3. If not admin:
     - Redirect to /login or /unauthorized
```

## 11. Current Implementation Scope

### 11.1 Fully Implemented (Ready for Frontend)

| Feature | Status | Notes |
|---------|--------|-------|
| Customer Authentication | âœ… Ready | Login, register, OTP, password reset |
| Admin Authentication | âœ… Ready | Via user system with admin role |
| Partner Authentication | âœ… Ready | Full lifecycle with state machine |
| Service Type CRUD | âœ… Ready | Admin create, update, delete |
| Partner Management | âœ… Ready | Approve, reject, suspend, reinstate |
| Service Item CRUD | âœ… Ready | Partner create, update, state changes |
| Service Item Moderation | âœ… Ready | Admin hide, show, archive |
| Public Service Browsing | âœ… Ready | List active items by partner |
| Search | âœ… Ready | Basic search with filters |

### 11.2 Backend Enhancements Needed

| Feature | Current Status | Recommendation |
|---------|----------------|----------------|
| Public Partner Profile | âš ï¸ Missing | Add `GET /api/services/:partnerId` for public partner details |
| Partner Listing by ServiceType | âš ï¸ Partial | Enhance search to return partner-level results |
| Featured Items | âš ï¸ Missing | Add `isFeatured` filter to search API |

---

## 12. Out of Scope

The following features are explicitly excluded from this specification:

| Feature | Reason |
|---------|--------|
| Booking UI | Booking backend not implemented |
| Payment UI | Payment backend not implemented |
| Availability Calendar | Booking backend not implemented |
| Pricing Rules | Payment backend not implemented |
| Reviews & Ratings | Not in current backend |
| Notifications | Not in current backend |
| File Upload UI | File upload mechanism not defined |
| Chat Support | Chat is for AI assistant, not customer support |
| Mobile App | Web-only specification |
| Analytics Dashboard | Not in current backend |

---

## Appendix A: API Base URLs

| Environment | Base URL |
|-------------|----------|
| Development | `http://localhost:5000/api` |
| Staging | TBD |
| Production | TBD |

## Appendix B: Authentication Headers

All authenticated requests must include:

```
Authorization: Bearer <access_token>
```

Token refresh:
- Access token expires: 15 minutes
- Refresh token expires: 7 days
- Refresh endpoint: `POST /api/refresh`

---

> **End of Specification**  
> This document provides complete frontend implementation guidance without requiring backend clarification for the defined scope.
